CANTEENS_NNP ._.

The_DT liberty_NN to_TO purchase_VB beer_NN freely_RB from_IN the_DT canteen_JJ seems_VBZ of_IN doubtful_JJ propriety_NN ,_, as_IN there_EX can_MD be_VB no_DT doubt_NN that_IN it_PRP leads_VBZ men_NNS to_TO think_VB that_IN they_PRP can_MD consume_VB any_DT quantity_NN of_IN the_DT liquor_NN with_IN impunity_NN ._.
